document model for the document to do the section wrapping.\n\nProblems with previous approach:\n1. Removal of sections that are inserted by parsoid and insertion\n   of CX Sections are done in sax parse step of document.\n2. The sax parsing model won't give sufficient forward context\n   to reliably determine the section tag end position. We had to\n   use many context holding variables.\n3. The template fragments that are connected using about attribute\n   should never be put in two different sections. To get this working\n   more context tracking variables were introduced. All added to\n   the fragility of the code\n4. span and div tags are sometimes block level tags and sometimes\n   inline tags based on the context. Added more complication\n\nNew approach:\n1. Delay the section wrapping till we build the linear document model\n2. Iterate the linear model, wrap the block level items with section tags\n3. If a tag has connection with previous section, insert the tag to\n   previous section.\n\nThis simplifies the sax parser and section wrap becomes a method in the\nlinear document just like segmentation.\n\nPrevious automated tests should pass.\n\nFor T202716, two classes were removed from the list of classes to remove\nfrom source article. Just removing without this refactoring was not possible\nsince the template fragements were going to two different sections.\n\nBug: T203780\nBug: T202716\nChange-Id: Ie9a2df909f4e62efaabbf69f26357e66542570b5","tree":{"sha":"6c63955e46d95c1a63f51ba637aef89a39db2cac","url":"https://api.github.com/repos/wikimedia/mediawiki-services-cxserver/git/trees/6c63955e46d95c1a63f51ba637aef89a39db2cac"},"url":"https://api.github.com/repos/wikimedia/mediawiki-services-cxserver/git/commits/e88c43c4588f3d1eae19051efa6c04dc60c5022d","comment_count":0,"verification":{"verified":true,"reason":"valid","signature":"-----BEGIN PGP SIGNATURE-----\n\niQFSBAABCgA8FiEE7yNXm75RSKgOspebUj3iiTTaC1oFAluaOw0eHHNhbnRob3No\nLnRob3R0aW5nYWxAZ21haWwuY29tAAoJEFI94ok02gtafdUH/iMABnd2lAGe/es/\n88UZV2sUARmMf8/vmBvJMCzdlS8PiuzPDrLqkCOxKzUalKfipNEQBjIRwbLAyVdQ\nfiTjKCUf9kEonuzNZvO7gtZpqJx06MFhyXxa1Svl044apYL0WGR/mxmDHpD5Ih74\nK6sDfpkbqyiJuZ9wvfKUzkiohqJoyQZ9fpFKe/Oz2xykCxodm7m9o2TJ0SlmTC4d\nVAHPxD0qMF8jLhviXL/MEIZBaj+O9YJzV8SY7t4Lz5iWDPqeC16zsmJgPX65wK1w\nvm8yAKomMBQR3dr8Q0OX8F/emdg9nHqeVZNJuPia0MgctoZrwCTUkCp8ritPpRPK\nHRZQIR0=\n=jQLs\n-----END PGP SIGNATURE-----","payload":"tree 6c63955e46d95c1a63f51ba637aef89a39db2cac\nparent 81d1a9711cb4308428cd856f5c2ce06c7d4d5b02\nauthor Santhosh Thottingal <santhosh.thottingal@gmail.com> 1536319551 +0530\ncommitter Santhosh Thottingal <santhosh.thottingal@gmail.com> 1536834314 +0530\n\nRewrite the section-wrap logic\n\nInstead of using the sax parser to wrap the sections, use the\nlinear document model for the document to do the section wrapping.\n\nProblems with previous approach:\n1. Removal of sections that are inserted by parsoid and insertion\n   of CX Sections are done in sax parse step of document.\n2. The sax parsing model won't give sufficient forward context\n   to reliably determine the section tag end position. We had to\n   use many context holding variables.\n3. The template fragments that are connected using about attribute\n   should never be put in two different sections. To get this working\n   more context tracking variables were introduced. All added to\n   the fragility of the code\n4. span and div tags are sometimes block level tags and sometimes\n   inline tags based on the context. Added more complication\n\nNew approach:\n1. Delay the section wrapping till we build the linear document model\n2. Iterate the linear model, wrap the block level items with section tags\n3. If a tag has connection with previous section, insert the tag to\n   previous section.\n\nThis simplifies the sax parser and section wrap becomes a method in the\nlinear document just like segmentation.\n\nPrevious automated tests should pass.\n\nFor T202716, two classes were removed from the list of classes to remove\nfrom source article.
